PROMPT  THIS SCRIPT CREATES AND POPULATES THE MOVIE DATABASE TABLES. Last updated Mar 2020.
PROMPT  Execute this script in ISQL JR.
PROMPT  When completed, do the following:
PROMPT  1. Clear the SQL statement box
PROMPT  2. Type this SQL statement and execute.   SELECT * FROM MOVIE2552
PROMPT     (This is how you see the rows in the Movie Table that script created)
PROMPT  3. Repeat similar SELECT statements for the ACTOR2552 and CASTING2552 tables.
PROMPT  .



PROMPT  Dropping any old versions of the Movie DB tables...

DROP TABLE CASTING2552; 
DROP TABLE ACTOR2552; 
DROP TABLE MOVIE2552; 
DROP TABLE COLOURTYPE2552; 
DROP TABLE RATING2552; 

PROMPT ****
PROMPT **** Create RATING Table...
CREATE TABLE RATING2552 (
  RATINGCODE   VARCHAR(2)
, SHORTDESC    VARCHAR(30)
, LONGDESC     VARCHAR(100)
, PRIMARY KEY  (RATINGCODE)
);
PROMPT **** The RATING table has been created

PROMPT ****
PROMPT **** Create COLOURTYPE Table...
CREATE TABLE COLOURTYPE2552 (
  COLOURCODE   VARCHAR(1)
, COLOURNAME   VARCHAR(30)
, PRIMARY KEY  (COLOURCODE)
);
PROMPT **** The COLOURTYPE table has been created

PROMPT ****-------------------------
PROMPT **** CREATE MOVIE TABLE ****
CREATE TABLE MOVIE2552 (
  MOVIENO      NUMBER(8) PRIMARY KEY
, TITLE        VARCHAR(100)
, RELYEAR      NUMBER(4)
, RUNTIME      NUMBER(4)
, RATINGCODE   VARCHAR(2)
, COLOURCODE   VARCHAR(1)
, TMDB_SCORE   NUMBER(3,1)
, TMDB_VOTES   NUMBER
, IMDB_ID      VARCHAR(12)
, FOREIGN KEY (RATINGCODE) references RATING2552
, FOREIGN KEY (COLOURCODE) references COLOURTYPE2552
);
PROMPT **** The MOVIE table has been created

PROMPT ****-------------------------
PROMPT **** CREATE ACTOR TABLE ****
CREATE TABLE ACTOR2552
(
  ACTORNO      NUMBER(8)
, FULLNAME     VARCHAR(100)
, GIVENNAME    VARCHAR(100)
, SURNAME      VARCHAR(100)
, GENDER       VARCHAR(1)
, BIRTHDATE    DATE
, BIRTHCOUNTRY VARCHAR(50)
, PASSWORD     VARCHAR(6)
, NOOFDOGS     NUMBER(2) 
, NOOFCATS     NUMBER(2) 
, PRIMARY KEY (ACTORNO)
);
PROMPT **** The ACTOR table has been created

PROMPT ****-------------------------
PROMPT **** CREATE CASTING TABLE ****
CREATE TABLE CASTING2552 (
  CASTID Number(8)
, ACTORNO NUMBER(8)
, MOVIENO NUMBER(8)
, PRIMARY KEY (CASTID)
, FOREIGN KEY (ACTORNO) references ACTOR2552
, FOREIGN KEY (MOVIENO) references MOVIE2552
);
PROMPT **** The CASTING table has been created

PROMPT ****
PROMPT **** Populating the RATING table...
INSERT INTO RATING2552 (ratingcode, shortdesc, longdesc) VALUES ('G', 'GENERAL','Suitable for all ages');
INSERT INTO RATING2552 (ratingcode, shortdesc, longdesc) VALUES ('M', 'MATURE (15+)','Recommended for mature audiences 15 years and over');
INSERT INTO RATING2552 (ratingcode, shortdesc, longdesc) VALUES ('MA', 'MATURE ACCOMPANIED (15+)','Persons under 15 years must be accompanied by a mature adult');
INSERT INTO RATING2552 (ratingcode, shortdesc, longdesc) VALUES ('PG', 'PARENTAL GUIDANCE','Parental guidance recommended for persons under 15 years');
INSERT INTO RATING2552 (ratingcode, shortdesc, longdesc) VALUES ('R', 'RESTRICTED (18+)','Restricted to mature adults 18 years and over');
PROMPT ****
PROMPT **** The RATING table has been populated with data

PROMPT ****
PROMPT **** Populating the COLOURTYPE table...
INSERT INTO COLOURTYPE2552 (colourcode, colourname) VALUES ('B', 'Black & White Movie');
INSERT INTO COLOURTYPE2552 (colourcode, colourname) VALUES ('C', 'Colour Movie');
PROMPT ****
PROMPT The COLOURTYPE table has been populated with data
